Introduction

The API documentation for Bookshelves to use endpoints with another app.

This documentation aims to provide all the information you need to work with our API.

As you scroll, you'll see code examples for working with the API in different programming languages in the dark area to the right (or as part of the content on mobile). You can switch the language used with the tabs at the top right (or from the nav menu at the top left on mobile).

Base URL

http://localhost:8000

Authenticating requests

This API is authenticated by sending an Authorization header with the value "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}".

All authenticated endpoints are marked with a requires authentication badge in the documentation below.

You can retrieve your token by visiting your dashboard and clicking Generate API token.

Laravel Sanctum

Account

GET Current user.

requires authentication

Route name: api.v1.profile

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/profile" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/profile"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/profile',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Example response (401):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
vary: Origin
 

{
    "message": "Unauthenticated."
}

Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/v1/profile/update

Body Parameters

name  string  

Must not be greater than 256 characters.

email  string  

Must be a valid email address. Must not be greater than 256 characters.

about  string optional  

Must not be greater than 2048 characters.

avatar  string optional  

Must not be greater than 2048 characters.

banner  string optional  

Must not be greater than 2048 characters.

use_gravatar  boolean  

display_favorites  boolean  

display_comments  boolean  

display_gender  boolean  

gender  string optional  

POST Delete current user.

requires authentication

Route name: api.v1.profile.delete

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/profile/delete" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"current_password\": \"udzrhwxympjleskygezcrqyrynsvatzdyadsgxjdhqtgckccblisryriytthuaniunkhscoomijsuhzruzhbrwwnecbtpuejakpnndowasohfwffvujwdfmzvzmlwjfnnriyobhxcamevlwdqrqhvlzgxrgbqisgqrmjjxtsfvuumfoqjxqcuxusryixjiyqmyyzklbmfdiseo\",
    \"confirm\": false
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/profile/delete"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "current_password": "udzrhwxympjleskygezcrqyrynsvatzdyadsgxjdhqtgckccblisryriytthuaniunkhscoomijsuhzruzhbrwwnecbtpuejakpnndowasohfwffvujwdfmzvzmlwjfnnriyobhxcamevlwdqrqhvlzgxrgbqisgqrmjjxtsfvuumfoqjxqcuxusryixjiyqmyyzklbmfdiseo",
    "confirm": false
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->post(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/profile/delete',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'json' => [
            'current_password' => 'udzrhwxympjleskygezcrqyrynsvatzdyadsgxjdhqtgckccblisryriytthuaniunkhscoomijsuhzruzhbrwwnecbtpuejakpnndowasohfwffvujwdfmzvzmlwjfnnriyobhxcamevlwdqrqhvlzgxrgbqisgqrmjjxtsfvuumfoqjxqcuxusryixjiyqmyyzklbmfdiseo',
            'confirm' => false,
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"

);

    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",

};

Request      

POST api/v1/password/update

Body Parameters

current_password  string  

Must not be greater than 256 characters.

password  string  

Must not be greater than 256 characters.

POST Login.

Route name: api.login

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/login" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"email\": \"edwina.mills@example.net\",
    \"password\": \"eaque\",
    \"remember\": false
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/login"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "email": "edwina.mills@example.net",
    "password": "eaque",
    "remember": false
};

fetch(url, {

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/authors?perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/authors"
);

const params = {
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/authors',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books?filter[languages]=en%2Cfr&sort=title_sort&perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books"
);

const params = {
    "filter[languages]": "en,fr",
    "sort": "title_sort",
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'filter[languages]'=> 'en,fr',
            'sort'=> 'title_sort',
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Depuis le 25 décembre 2008, le Noël de Sang, les autorités maintenaient la population parisienne dans une terreur permanente. Les familles n'avaient pas pu enterrer leurs morts, ensevelis dans de gigantesques fosses communes creusées dans les campagnes environnantes. Pas de sépulture pour ceux qui avaient osé défier le pouvoir royal. Vidé d'une grande partie de sa population, Paris s'était replié sur lui-même et enveloppé dans une résignation morne. Présentation de l'éditeurTrop bête d'échouer si près du but. Il ne chercha pas à contourner les dernières flaques, il fila droit devant lui, soulevant par instants de grandes gerbes d'eau. Lorsqu'il atteignit enfin la rive opposée, il fut pris d'un étourdissement, se jeta sur le sol et reprit son souffle. La traversée du bras de mer lui avait pris en grande partie ses dernières forces. [...] Il frémit de joie lorsqu'il prit conscience qu'il foulait désormais le même sol que Clara. Clara est enlevée pour être mariée de force à un riche industriel de la Nouvelle-France, l'un des cinq royaumes d'Amérique du Nord. Jean se lance dans une folle recherche qui lui fera traverser l'Atlantique au fond de la cale du paquebot Henri-VII, puis effectuer un long et dangereux périple à travers une Amérique hostile. Arrivera-t-il à temps pour la délivrer ? De son côté, Elan Gris, un jeune Lakota, s'enfuit de sa réserve pour tenter de gagner le pays fabuleux de ses visions...",

Request      

GET api/v1/books/{author_slug}/{book_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author books' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to books' list and not authors' list, example: bordage-pierre

book_slug  string  

slug of book in meta.slug books' list, example: ceux-qui-revent-fr

GET Book collection related entries.

WITH PAGINATION

Get all Series/Books related to selected Book from Tag/Genre.

Route name: api.v1.books.related

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books/related/troisi-licia/la-secte-des-assassins-fr?perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books/related/troisi-licia/la-secte-des-assassins-fr"
);

const params = {
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/books/related/troisi-licia/la-secte-des-assassins-fr',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

GET Author ZIP.

Content-Type application/octet-stream

Download Author ZIP, find by slug of author.

Route name: api.v1.download.author

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/download/author/howey-hugh" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/octet-stream" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/download/author/howey-hugh"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/octet-stream",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/download/author/howey-hugh',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/octet-stream',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Example response (200):

Show headers 
content-disposition: attachment; filename="howey-hugh-tsysqmeg.zip"
content-type: application/octet-stream
cache-control: no-cache, private
x-ratelimit-limit: 5000
x-ratelimit-remaining: 4977
vary: Origin
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

GET api/v1/download/author/{author_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.slug authors' list, example: howey-hugh

Favorite

GET Favorites by user.

requires authentication

Route name: api.v1.favorites.user

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/favorites/{user_id}" \
    --header "Authorization: Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/favorites/{user_id}"
);

const headers = {
    "Authorization": "Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}",
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/favorites/{user_id}',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Authorization' => 'Bearer {YOUR_AUTH_KEY}',
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Request      

GET api/v1/enums

GET Count.

Get count of entities for a selected collection. Available for Book, Serie and Author.

Route name: api.v1.count

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/count?entities=author%2Cbook%2Cserie&languages=fr%2Cen" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/count"
);

const params = {
    "entities": "author,book,serie",
    "languages": "fr,en",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/count',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'entities'=> 'author,book,serie',
            'languages'=> 'fr,en',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Example response (200):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 5000
x-ratelimit-remaining: 4981
vary: Origin
 

{
    "data": {
        "entities": {
            "author": 62,
            "book": 593,
            "serie": 85
        },
        "languages": {
            "fr": 476,
            "en": 0
        }
    }
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:

POST Send submission.

Route name: api.v1.submission.send

Example request:
curl --request POST \
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/submission" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json" \
    --data "{
    \"name\": \"voluptates\",
    \"email\": \"pnitzsche@example.com\",
    \"honeypot\": false,
    \"message\": \"\"
}"

const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/submission"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

let body = {
    "name": "voluptates",
    "email": "pnitzsche@example.com",
    "honeypot": false,
    "message": ""
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "POST",
    headers,
    body: JSON.stringify(body),
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->post(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/submission',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'json' => [
            'name' => 'voluptates',
            'email' => 'pnitzsche@example.com',
            'honeypot' => false,
            'message' => '',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Example response (422):

Show headers 
cache-control: no-cache, private
content-type: application/json
x-ratelimit-limit: 5000
x-ratelimit-remaining: 4976
vary: Origin
 

{
    "message": "The email must be a valid email address. (and 1 more error)",
    "errors": {
        "email": [
            "The email must be a valid email address."
        ],
        "message": [
            "The message field is required."
        ]
    }
}
Received response:
Request failed with error:

Request      

POST api/v1/submission

Body Parameters

name  string  

email  string  

Must be a valid email address.

honeypot  boolean  

message  string  

Must be at least 15 characters.

Search

GET Search.

Search full-text into authors, books & series.

Route name: api.v1.search.index

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/search?q=soleil+bl%C3%AAme" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/search"
);

const params = {
    "q": "soleil bl√™me",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/search',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'q'=> 'soleil bl√™me',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

GET List series.

WITH PAGINATION

Get all series ordered by title & serie_title.

Route name: api.v1.series.index

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series?filter[languages]=en%2Cfr&perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series"
);

const params = {
    "filter[languages]": "en,fr",
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'filter[languages]'=> 'en,fr',
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Request      

GET api/v1/series

Query Parameters

filter[languages]  string optional  

To select specific lang, null by default.

perPage  int optional  

Number of entities to return in a page.

page  int optional  

Page number to return, 1 by default

Response

Response Fields

data  object[]  

List of series.

links  object  

Links to get other pages.

meta  object  

Metadata about pagination.

GET Serie resource.

Get details of Serie model, find by slug of serie and slug of author.

Route name: api.v1.series.show

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/fforde-jasper/thursday-next-fr" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/fforde-jasper/thursday-next-fr"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/fforde-jasper/thursday-next-fr',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Request      

GET api/v1/series/{author_slug}/{serie_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author series' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to series' list and not authors' list, example: fforde-jasper

serie_slug  string  

slug of serie in meta.slug series' list, example: thursday-next-fr

GET Book collection of Serie.

Books list from one Serie, find by slug.

Route name: api.v1.series.show.books

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/herbert-frank/dune-fr?perPage=5&page=1" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/herbert-frank/dune-fr"
);

const params = {
    "perPage": "5",
    "page": "1",
};
Object.keys(params)
    .forEach(key => url.searchParams.append(key, params[key]));

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/series/books/herbert-frank/dune-fr',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
        'query' => [
            'perPage'=> '5',
            'page'=> '1',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));

Request      

GET api/v1/series/books/{author_slug}/{serie_slug}

URL Parameters

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author series' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to series' list and not authors' list, example: herbert-frank

serie_slug  string  

slug of serie in meta.slug series' list, example: dune-fr

Query Parameters

perPage  int optional  

Number of entities to return in a page.

page  int optional  

Page number to return, 1 by default

Request      

GET api/v1/series/books/{volume}/{author_slug}/{serie_slug}

URL Parameters

volume  int  

Current volume

author_slug  string  

slug of author in meta.author series' list, in case of multiple authors, default author is selected so you need to refer to series' list and not authors' list, example: arnaud-georges-jean

serie_slug  string  

slug of serie in meta.slug series' list, example: la-compagnie-des-glaces-fr

Tag

GET Tag collection.

Get all Tags ordered by 'name'.

Route name: api.v1.tags.index

Example request:
curl --request GET \
    --get "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/tags" \
    --header "Content-Type: application/json" \
    --header "Accept: application/json"
const url = new URL(
    "http://localhost:8000/api/v1/tags"
);

const headers = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Accept": "application/json",
};

fetch(url, {
    method: "GET",
    headers,
}).then(response => response.json());
$client = new \GuzzleHttp\Client();
$response = $client->get(
    'http://localhost:8000/api/v1/tags',
    [
        'headers' => [
            'Content-Type' => 'application/json',
            'Accept' => 'application/json',
        ],
    ]
);
$body = $response->getBody();
print_r(json_decode((string) $body));
